21/** @file
22 * @short Upipe higher-level module muxing elementary streams in a TS
23 * Four parts in this file:
24 * @list
25 * @item psi_pid structure, which handles PSI multiplexing using ts_psi_join
26 * @item input sink pipe, which is returned to the application, and
27 * represents an elementary stream; it sets up the ts_encaps inner pipe
28 * @item program join pipe, which is returned to the application, and
29 * represents a program
30 * @item mux source pipe which sets up the ts_psig, and ts_sig inner pipes
31 *
32 * Normative references:
33 * - ISO/IEC 13818-1:2007(E) (MPEG-2 Systems)
34 * - ETSI EN 300 468 V1.13.1 (2012-08) (SI in DVB systems)
35 * - ETSI TR 101 211 V1.9.1 (2009-06) (Guidelines of SI in DVB systems)
36 * - ETSI TS 103 197 V1.3.1 (2003-01) (DVB SimulCrypt)
37 */
38

163/** @internal @This is the private context of a ts_mux manager. */
164struct upipe_ts_mux_mgr {
165 /** refcount management structure */
166 struct urefcount urefcount;
167
168 /* inputs */

170 struct upipe_mgr *ts_encaps_mgr;
171
172 /* PSI */
173 /** pointer to ts_psi_join manager */
174 struct upipe_mgr *ts_psi_join_mgr;
175 /** pointer to ts_psig manager */
176 struct upipe_mgr *ts_psig_mgr;
177 /** pointer to ts_sig manager */
178 struct upipe_mgr *ts_sig_mgr;
179
180 /* ES */
181 /** pointer to ts_tstd manager */
182 struct upipe_mgr *ts_tstd_mgr;
183
184 /** public upipe_mgr structure */
185 struct upipe_mgr mgr;
186};

*upipe, struct urequest *urequest) { struct upipe_ts_mux *s =

(urequest)); if (__builtin_expect(!!(s->psig != ((void*)0)
),1)) return upipe_unregister_request(s->psig, urequest); return
UBASE_ERR_NONE; } static int upipe_ts_mux_provide_bin_proxy(
struct urequest *urequest, va_list args) { struct urequest *upstream
= (struct urequest *)(urequest)->opaque; return urequest_provide_va
(upstream, args); } static int upipe_ts_mux_alloc_bin_proxy(struct
upipe *upipe, struct urequest *urequest) { struct urequest *

urequest_init(proxy, urequest->type, uref, upipe_ts_mux_provide_bin_proxy
, (urequest_free_func)free); return upipe_ts_mux_register_bin_request

*s = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe); struct uchain *uchain, *

*s = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe); switch (command) { case

(args, struct urequest *); return upipe_ts_mux_alloc_bin_proxy
(upipe, request); } case UPIPE_UNREGISTER_REQUEST: { struct urequest

upipe_ts_mux_free_bin_proxy(upipe, request); } case UPIPE_SET_FLOW_DEF

(struct upipe *upipe) { struct upipe_ts_mux *s = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe
(upipe); upipe_release(s->psig); }

375/** @internal @This is the private context of a program of a ts_mux pipe. */
376struct upipe_ts_mux_program {
377 /** real refcount management structure */
378 struct urefcount urefcount_real;
379 /** refcount management structure */
380 struct urefcount urefcount;
381 /** structure for double-linked lists */
382 struct uchain uchain;
383
384 /** SID */
385 uint16_t sid;
386 /** PMT PID */
387 uint16_t pmt_pid;
388
389 /** proxy probe */
390 struct uprobe probe;
391 /** list of input bin requests */
392 struct uchain input_request_list;
393
394 /** pointer to ts_psig_program */
395 struct upipe *psig_program;
396 /** psi_pid structure for PMT */
397 struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid *psi_pid_pmt;
398
399 /** pointer to ts_sig_service */
400 struct upipe *sig_service;
401
402 /** calculated required octetrate including overheads and PMT */
403 uint64_t required_octetrate;
404
405 /** interval between PMTs */
406 uint64_t pmt_interval;
407 /** interval between PCRs */
408 uint64_t pcr_interval;
409 /** interval between EITs */
410 uint64_t eit_interval;
411 /** maximum retention delay */
412 uint64_t max_delay;
413
414 /** input flow definition */
415 struct uref *flow_def_input;
416 /** list of inputs */
417 struct uchain inputs;
418
419 /** manager to create inputs */
420 struct upipe_mgr input_mgr;
421
422 /** public upipe structure */
423 struct upipe upipe;
424};

444/** @internal @This defines the role of an input wrt. PCR management and
445 * scheduling. */
446enum upipe_ts_mux_input_type {
447 /** video */
448 UPIPE_TS_MUX_INPUT_VIDEO,
449 /** audio */
450 UPIPE_TS_MUX_INPUT_AUDIO,
451 /** other (unsuitable for PCR) */
452 UPIPE_TS_MUX_INPUT_OTHER
453};
454
455/** @internal @This is the private context of an output of a ts_mux_program
456 * subpipe. */
457struct upipe_ts_mux_input {
458 /** real refcount management structure */
459 struct urefcount urefcount_real;
460 /** refcount management structure */
461 struct urefcount urefcount;
462 /** structure for double-linked lists */
463 struct uchain uchain;
464
465 /** true if the input is in the process of being deleted */
466 bool_Bool deleted;
467 /** input type */
468 enum upipe_ts_mux_input_type input_type;
469 /** PID */
470 uint16_t pid;
471 /** octet rate */
472 uint64_t octetrate;
473 /** buffering duration */
474 uint64_t buffer_duration;
475 /** true if the output is used for PCR */
476 bool_Bool pcr;
477 /** calculated required octetrate including overheads */
478 uint64_t required_octetrate;
479
480 /** proxy probe */
481 struct uprobe probe;
482 /** list of input bin requests */
483 struct uchain input_request_list;
484 /** pointer to ts_tstd */
485 struct upipe *tstd;
486 /** pointer to ts_encaps */
487 struct upipe *encaps;
488 /** probe passed to ts_encaps */
489 struct uprobe encaps_probe;
490 /** cr_sys of the next packet */
491 uint64_t cr_sys;
492 /** dts_sys of the next packet */
493 uint64_t dts_sys;
494 /** cr_sys of the next PCR */
495 uint64_t pcr_sys;
496 /** true if the input is ready to output packet */
497 bool_Bool ready;
498
499 /** maximum retention delay */
500 uint64_t max_delay;
501 /** number of access units per second */
502 struct urational au_per_sec;
503 /** original number of access units per second before aggregation */
504 struct urational original_au_per_sec;
505
506 /** public upipe structure */
507 struct upipe upipe;
508};

( upipe_ts_mux_input_from_uchain(u->next)); return UBASE_ERR_NONE
; } static __attribute__ ((unused)) void upipe_ts_mux_program_throw_sub_inputs
(struct upipe *upipe, int event, ...) { struct upipe_ts_mux_program
*s = upipe_ts_mux_program_from_upipe(upipe); struct uchain *
uchain; struct upipe_ts_mux_input *sub = ((void*)0); for ((uchain
) = (&s->inputs)->next; (uchain) != (&s->inputs
); (uchain) = (uchain)->next) { if (sub != ((void*)0)) upipe_release
( upipe_ts_mux_input_to_upipe(sub)); sub = upipe_ts_mux_input_from_uchain
(uchain); upipe_use( upipe_ts_mux_input_to_upipe(sub)); va_list
args; __builtin_va_start(args, event); upipe_throw_va( upipe_ts_mux_input_to_upipe
(sub), event, args); __builtin_va_end(args); } if (sub != ((void
*)0)) upipe_release( upipe_ts_mux_input_to_upipe(sub)); } static
void upipe_ts_mux_program_clean_sub_inputs(struct upipe *upipe
) { }

525/*
526 * psi_pid structure handling
527 */
528
529/** @internal @This is the context of a PID carrying PSI of a ts_mux pipe. */
530struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid {
531 /** reference count */
532 unsigned int refcount;
533 /** structure for double-linked lists */
534 struct uchain uchain;
535
536 /** PID */
537 uint16_t pid;
538 /** pointer to upipe_ts_mux pipe */
539 struct upipe *upipe;
540
541 /** pointer to psi_join inner pipe */
542 struct upipe *psi_join;
543 /** pointer to encaps inner pipe */
544 struct upipe *encaps;
545
546 /** probe passed to psi_join */
547 struct uprobe join_probe;
548 /** probe passed to encaps */
549 struct uprobe encaps_probe;
550 /** octetrate of the PID */
551 uint64_t octetrate;
552 /** cr_sys of the next table */
553 uint64_t cr_sys;
554 /** dts_sys of the next table */
555 uint64_t dts_sys;
556};
557
558UBASE_FROM_TO(upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid, uchain, uchain, uchain)static __attribute__ ((unused)) inline struct uchain * upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_to_uchain
(struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid *s) { return &s->uchain; }
static __attribute__ ((unused)) inline struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid
* upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_from_uchain(struct uchain *sub) { return
({ const typeof( ((struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid *)0)->uchain
) *_mptr = (sub); (struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid *)( (char *)_mptr
- __builtin_offsetof(struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid, uchain) );
}); }
559
560/** @internal @This catches the events from psi_join inner pipes.
561 *
562 * @param uprobe pointer to the probe in upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid
563 * @param inner pointer to the inner pipe
564 * @param event event triggered by the subpipe
565 * @param args arguments of the event
566 * @return an error code
567 */
568static int upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_join_probe(struct uprobe *uprobe,
569 struct upipe *inner,
570 int event, va_list args)
571{
572 struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid *psi_pid =
573 container_of(uprobe, struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid, join_probe)({ const typeof( ((struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid *)0)->join_probe
) *_mptr = (uprobe); (struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid *)( (char *
)_mptr - __builtin_offsetof(struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid, join_probe
) );});
574
575 if (event == UPROBE_NEED_OUTPUT)
576 return UBASE_ERR_UNHANDLED;
577 if (event != UPROBE_NEW_FLOW_DEF)
578 return upipe_throw_proxy(psi_pid->upipe, inner, event, args);
579
580 struct uref *flow_def = va_arg(args, struct uref *)__builtin_va_arg(args, struct uref *);
581 uint64_t octetrate = 0;
582 uref_block_flow_get_octetrate(flow_def, &octetrate);
583 uint64_t section_interval = 0;
584 uref_ts_flow_get_psi_section_interval(flow_def, &section_interval);
585 if (section_interval)
586 /* pointer_field + padding overhead */
587 octetrate += (uint64_t)(TS_SIZE188 - TS_HEADER_SIZE4) * UCLOCK_FREQ27000000UL /
588 section_interval;
589 /* TS header overhead */
590 octetrate += TS_HEADER_SIZE4 * octetrate / (TS_SIZE188 - TS_HEADER_SIZE4);
591 /* round down to nearest TS packet - this is to avoid bouncing up and
592 * down around a middle value */
593 octetrate -= octetrate % TS_SIZE188;
594 if (octetrate != psi_pid->octetrate) {
595 psi_pid->octetrate = octetrate;
596 upipe_ts_mux_update(psi_pid->upipe);
597 }
598 return UBASE_ERR_NONE;
599}
600
601/** @internal @This catches the events from encaps inner pipes.
602 *
603 * @param uprobe pointer to the probe in upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid
604 * @param inner pointer to the inner pipe
605 * @param event event triggered by the subpipe
606 * @param args arguments of the event
607 * @return an error code
608 */
609static int upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_encaps_probe(struct uprobe *uprobe,
610 struct upipe *inner,
611 int event, va_list args)
612{
613 struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid *psi_pid =
614 container_of(uprobe, struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid, encaps_probe)({ const typeof( ((struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid *)0)->encaps_probe
) *_mptr = (uprobe); (struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid *)( (char *
)_mptr - __builtin_offsetof(struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid, encaps_probe
) );});
615
616 if (event == UPROBE_NEED_OUTPUT)
617 return UBASE_ERR_UNHANDLED;
618 if (event != UPROBE_TS_ENCAPS_STATUS)
619 return upipe_throw_proxy(psi_pid->upipe, inner, event, args);
620
621 UBASE_SIGNATURE_CHECK(args, UPIPE_TS_ENCAPS_SIGNATURE){ if (__builtin_va_arg(args, unsigned int) != (((uint32_t)'t'
) | (((uint32_t)'s') << 8) | (((uint32_t)'e') << 16
) | (((uint32_t)'c') << 24))) return UBASE_ERR_UNHANDLED
; }
622
623 psi_pid->cr_sys = va_arg(args, uint64_t)__builtin_va_arg(args, uint64_t);
624 psi_pid->dts_sys = va_arg(args, uint64_t)__builtin_va_arg(args, uint64_t);
625 return UBASE_ERR_NONE;
626}
627

709
710/** @internal @This finds a psi_pid by its PID.
711 *
712 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
713 * @param pid PID
714 * @return pointer to substructure
715 */
716static struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid *
717 upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_find(struct upipe *upipe, uint16_t pid)
718{
719 struct upipe_ts_mux *upipe_ts_mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
720 struct uchain *uchain;
721 ulist_foreach (&upipe_ts_mux->psi_pids, uchain)for ((uchain) = (&upipe_ts_mux->psi_pids)->next; (uchain
) != (&upipe_ts_mux->psi_pids); (uchain) = (uchain)->
next) {
722 struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid *psi_pid =
723 upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_from_uchain(uchain);
724 if (psi_pid->pid == pid)
725 return psi_pid;
726 }
727 return NULL((void*)0);
728}
729
730/** @internal @This marks a PID as being used for PSI, optionally allocates
731 * the substructure, and increments the refcount.
732 *
733 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
734 * @param pid PID
735 * @return pointer to substructure
736 */
737static struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid *
738 upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_use(struct upipe *upipe, uint16_t pid)
739{
740 struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid *psi_pid =
741 upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_find(upipe, pid);
742 if (psi_pid == NULL((void*)0))
743 return upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_alloc(upipe, pid);
744
745 psi_pid->refcount++;
746 return psi_pid;
747}
748
749/** @internal @This releases a PID from being used for PSI, optionally
750 * freeing allocated resources.
751 *
752 * @param psi_pid psi_pid structure
753 */
754static void upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_release(struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid *psi_pid)
755{
756 if (psi_pid == NULL((void*)0))
757 return;
758 psi_pid->refcount--;
759 if (!psi_pid->refcount) {
760 ulist_delete(upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_to_uchain(psi_pid));
761 upipe_release(psi_pid->psi_join);
762 upipe_release(psi_pid->encaps);
763 uprobe_clean(&psi_pid->encaps_probe);
764 free(psi_pid);
765 }
766}
767
768
769/*
770 * upipe_ts_mux_input structure handling (derived from upipe structure)
771 */
772
773/** @internal @This catches the events from inner pipes.
774 *
775 * @param uprobe pointer to the probe in upipe_ts_mux_input
776 * @param inner pointer to the inner pipe
777 * @param event event triggered by the subpipe
778 * @param args arguments of the event
779 * @return an error code
780 */
781static int upipe_ts_mux_input_probe(struct uprobe *uprobe, struct upipe *inner,
782 int event, va_list args)
783{
784 struct upipe_ts_mux_input *upipe_ts_mux_input =

1253/** @This frees a upipe.
1254 *
1255 * @param urefcount_real pointer to urefcount_real structure
1256 */
1257static void upipe_ts_mux_input_free(struct urefcount *urefcount_real)
1258{
1259 struct upipe_ts_mux_input *upipe_ts_mux_input =
1260 upipe_ts_mux_input_from_urefcount_real(urefcount_real);
1261 struct upipe *upipe = upipe_ts_mux_input_to_upipe(upipe_ts_mux_input);
1262 struct upipe_ts_mux_program *program =
1263 upipe_ts_mux_program_from_input_mgr(upipe->mgr);
1264
1265 upipe_ts_mux_input_clean_sub(upipe);
1266 if (!upipe_single(upipe_ts_mux_program_to_upipe(program)))
1267 upipe_ts_mux_program_change(upipe_ts_mux_program_to_upipe(program));
1268
1269 upipe_throw_dead(upipe);
1270
1271 uprobe_clean(&upipe_ts_mux_input->probe);
1272 uprobe_clean(&upipe_ts_mux_input->encaps_probe);
1273 urefcount_clean(urefcount_real);
1274 upipe_ts_mux_input_clean_urefcount(upipe);
1275 upipe_ts_mux_input_free_void(upipe);
1276}

1440/** @This calculates the total octetrate used by a program and updates the
1441 * mux.
1442 *
1443 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
1444 */
1445static void upipe_ts_mux_program_update(struct upipe *upipe)
1446{

1448 upipe_ts_mux_program_from_upipe(upipe);

1453 ((UCLOCK_FREQ27000000UL + upipe_ts_mux_program->pcr_interval - 1) /
1454 upipe_ts_mux_program->pcr_interval);

1457 ulist_foreach (&upipe_ts_mux_program->inputs, uchain)for ((uchain) = (&upipe_ts_mux_program->inputs)->next
; (uchain) != (&upipe_ts_mux_program->inputs); (uchain
) = (uchain)->next) {
1458 struct upipe_ts_mux_input *input =
1459 upipe_ts_mux_input_from_uchain(uchain);
1460 required_octetrate += input->required_octetrate;
1461 }

1463 upipe_ts_mux_program->required_octetrate = required_octetrate;
1464
1465 struct upipe_ts_mux *upipe_ts_mux =
1466 upipe_ts_mux_from_program_mgr(upipe->mgr);
1467 upipe_ts_mux_update(upipe_ts_mux_to_upipe(upipe_ts_mux));
1468}

1470/** @This is called when the program definition is changed (input added or
1471 * deleted).
1472 *
1473 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
1474 */
1475static void upipe_ts_mux_program_change(struct upipe *upipe)
1476{
1477 struct upipe_ts_mux_program *upipe_ts_mux_program =
1478 upipe_ts_mux_program_from_upipe(upipe);
1479 uint64_t pcr_pid = UNDEF_PCR8191, old_pcr_pid = UNDEF_PCR8191;
1480 struct upipe_ts_mux_input *pcr_input = NULL((void*)0), *old_pcr_input = NULL((void*)0);
1481
1482 struct uchain *uchain;
1483 ulist_foreach (&upipe_ts_mux_program->inputs, uchain)for ((uchain) = (&upipe_ts_mux_program->inputs)->next
; (uchain) != (&upipe_ts_mux_program->inputs); (uchain
) = (uchain)->next) {
1484 struct upipe_ts_mux_input *input =
1485 upipe_ts_mux_input_from_uchain(uchain);
1486 if (input->pcr) {
1487 old_pcr_pid = input->pid;
1488 old_pcr_input = input;
1489 }
1490 if (input->input_type == UPIPE_TS_MUX_INPUT_OTHER)
1491 continue;
1492 if (pcr_input == NULL((void*)0) ||
1493 (pcr_input->input_type == UPIPE_TS_MUX_INPUT_AUDIO &&
1494 input->input_type == UPIPE_TS_MUX_INPUT_VIDEO)) {
1495 pcr_pid = input->pid;
1496 pcr_input = input;
1497 }
1498 }
1499
1500 if (pcr_pid != old_pcr_pid) {
1501 if (old_pcr_pid != UNDEF_PCR8191) {
1502 old_pcr_input->pcr = false0;
1503 if (old_pcr_input->encaps != NULL((void*)0))
1504 upipe_ts_mux_set_pcr_interval(old_pcr_input->encaps, 0);
1505 }
1506
1507 if (pcr_pid != UNDEF_PCR8191) {
1508 pcr_input->pcr = true1;
1509 if (pcr_input->encaps != NULL((void*)0))
1510 upipe_ts_mux_set_pcr_interval(pcr_input->encaps,
1511 upipe_ts_mux_program->pcr_interval);
1512 }
1513 upipe_ts_psig_program_set_pcr_pid(upipe_ts_mux_program->psig_program,
1514 pcr_pid);
1515 }
1516}
1517
1518/** @internal @This sets the initial cr_prog of the program to the given value.
1519 *
1520 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
1521 * @param cr_prog initial cr_prog value
1522 */
1523static void upipe_ts_mux_program_init_cr_prog(struct upipe *upipe,
1524 uint64_t cr_prog)
1525{
1526 struct upipe_ts_mux_program *program =
1527 upipe_ts_mux_program_from_upipe(upipe);
1528 uint64_t min_cr_sys = UINT64_MAX(18446744073709551615UL);
1529
1530 struct uchain *uchain;
1531 ulist_foreach (&program->inputs, uchain)for ((uchain) = (&program->inputs)->next; (uchain) !=
(&program->inputs); (uchain) = (uchain)->next) {
1532 struct upipe_ts_mux_input *input =
1533 upipe_ts_mux_input_from_uchain(uchain);
1534 if (input->cr_sys < min_cr_sys)
1535 min_cr_sys = input->cr_sys;
1536 }
1537
1538 ulist_foreach (&program->inputs, uchain)for ((uchain) = (&program->inputs)->next; (uchain) !=
(&program->inputs); (uchain) = (uchain)->next) {
1539 struct upipe_ts_mux_input *input =
1540 upipe_ts_mux_input_from_uchain(uchain);
1541 upipe_ts_mux_set_cr_prog(input->encaps,
1542 cr_prog + input->cr_sys - min_cr_sys);
1543 }
1544}
1545
1546/** @internal @This sets the input flow definition.
1547 *
1548 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
1549 * @param flow_def flow definition packet
1550 * @return an error code
1551 */
1552static int upipe_ts_mux_program_set_flow_def(struct upipe *upipe,
1553 struct uref *flow_def)
1554{
1555 if (flow_def == NULL((void*)0))
1556 return UBASE_ERR_INVALID;
1557
1558 struct upipe_ts_mux_program *program =
1559 upipe_ts_mux_program_from_upipe(upipe);
1560 struct upipe_ts_mux *mux =
1561 upipe_ts_mux_from_program_mgr(upipe->mgr);
1562 UBASE_RETURN(uref_flow_match_def(flow_def, "void."))do { int ubase_err_tmp = uref_flow_match_def(flow_def, "void."
); if (__builtin_expect(!!(!ubase_check(ubase_err_tmp)),0)) return
ubase_err_tmp; } while (0);
1563 struct uref *flow_def_dup;
1564 if (unlikely((flow_def_dup = uref_dup(flow_def)) == NULL)__builtin_expect(!!((flow_def_dup = uref_dup(flow_def)) == ((
void*)0)),0))
1565 return UBASE_ERR_ALLOC;
1566
1567 uint64_t sid = 0;
1568 uref_flow_get_id(flow_def, &sid);
1569 if (sid == 0) {
1570 do {
1571 sid = mux->sid_auto++;
1572 } while (upipe_ts_mux_find_sid(upipe_ts_mux_to_upipe(mux),
1573 sid));
1574 if (sid >= MAX_SIDS(65535)) {
1575 uref_free(flow_def_dup);
1576 return UBASE_ERR_BUSY;
1577 } else
1578 UBASE_FATAL(upipe, uref_flow_set_id(flow_def_dup, sid))do { int ubase_err_tmp = uref_flow_set_id(flow_def_dup, sid);
if (__builtin_expect(!!(!ubase_check(ubase_err_tmp)),0)) do {
uprobe_err_va((upipe)->uprobe, upipe, "fatal error at %s:%d (0x%x)"
, "upipe_ts_mux.c", 1578, ubase_err_tmp); uprobe_throw((upipe
)->uprobe, upipe, UPROBE_FATAL, ubase_err_tmp); } while (0
); } while (0);;
1579 }
1580
1581 uint64_t pid = 0;
1582 uref_ts_flow_get_pid(flow_def, &pid);
1583 if (pid == 0) {
1584 do {
1585 pid = mux->pid_auto++;
1586 } while (upipe_ts_mux_find_pid(upipe_ts_mux_to_upipe(mux),
1587 pid));
1588 if (pid >= MAX_PIDS8192) {
1589 uref_free(flow_def_dup);
1590 return UBASE_ERR_BUSY;
1591 } else
1592 UBASE_FATAL(upipe, uref_ts_flow_set_pid(flow_def_dup, pid))do { int ubase_err_tmp = uref_ts_flow_set_pid(flow_def_dup, pid
); if (__builtin_expect(!!(!ubase_check(ubase_err_tmp)),0)) do
{ uprobe_err_va((upipe)->uprobe, upipe, "fatal error at %s:%d (0x%x)"
, "upipe_ts_mux.c", 1592, ubase_err_tmp); uprobe_throw((upipe
)->uprobe, upipe, UPROBE_FATAL, ubase_err_tmp); } while (0
); } while (0);;
1593 }
1594
1595 if (program->pmt_pid != pid) {
1596 upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_release(program->psi_pid_pmt);
1597 program->psi_pid_pmt =
1598 upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_use(upipe_ts_mux_to_upipe(mux), pid);
1599 struct upipe *psi_join;
1600 if (unlikely((psi_join =__builtin_expect(!!((psi_join = upipe_void_alloc_output_sub(program
->psig_program, program->psi_pid_pmt->psi_join, uprobe_pfx_alloc
( uprobe_use(&program->probe), UPROBE_LOG_VERBOSE, "pmt psi_join"
))) == ((void*)0)),0)
1601 upipe_void_alloc_output_sub(program->psig_program,__builtin_expect(!!((psi_join = upipe_void_alloc_output_sub(program
->psig_program, program->psi_pid_pmt->psi_join, uprobe_pfx_alloc
( uprobe_use(&program->probe), UPROBE_LOG_VERBOSE, "pmt psi_join"
))) == ((void*)0)),0)
1602 program->psi_pid_pmt->psi_join,__builtin_expect(!!((psi_join = upipe_void_alloc_output_sub(program
->psig_program, program->psi_pid_pmt->psi_join, uprobe_pfx_alloc
( uprobe_use(&program->probe), UPROBE_LOG_VERBOSE, "pmt psi_join"
))) == ((void*)0)),0)
1603 uprobe_pfx_alloc(__builtin_expect(!!((psi_join = upipe_void_alloc_output_sub(program
->psig_program, program->psi_pid_pmt->psi_join, uprobe_pfx_alloc
( uprobe_use(&program->probe), UPROBE_LOG_VERBOSE, "pmt psi_join"
))) == ((void*)0)),0)
1604 uprobe_use(&program->probe),__builtin_expect(!!((psi_join = upipe_void_alloc_output_sub(program
->psig_program, program->psi_pid_pmt->psi_join, uprobe_pfx_alloc
( uprobe_use(&program->probe), UPROBE_LOG_VERBOSE, "pmt psi_join"
))) == ((void*)0)),0)
1605 UPROBE_LOG_VERBOSE,__builtin_expect(!!((psi_join = upipe_void_alloc_output_sub(program
->psig_program, program->psi_pid_pmt->psi_join, uprobe_pfx_alloc
( uprobe_use(&program->probe), UPROBE_LOG_VERBOSE, "pmt psi_join"
))) == ((void*)0)),0)
1606 "pmt psi_join"))) == NULL)__builtin_expect(!!((psi_join = upipe_void_alloc_output_sub(program
->psig_program, program->psi_pid_pmt->psi_join, uprobe_pfx_alloc
( uprobe_use(&program->probe), UPROBE_LOG_VERBOSE, "pmt psi_join"
))) == ((void*)0)),0))
1607 upipe_throw_fatal(upipe, UBASE_ERR_ALLOC)do { uprobe_err_va((upipe)->uprobe, upipe, "fatal error at %s:%d (0x%x)"
, "upipe_ts_mux.c", 1607, UBASE_ERR_ALLOC); uprobe_throw((upipe
)->uprobe, upipe, UPROBE_FATAL, UBASE_ERR_ALLOC); } while (
0);
1608 upipe_release(psi_join);
1609 }
1610
1611 uref_free(program->flow_def_input);
1612 program->flow_def_input = flow_def_dup;
1613
1614 if (!ubase_check(upipe_set_flow_def(program->psig_program, flow_def_dup))) {
1615 uref_free(flow_def_dup);
1616 return UBASE_ERR_INVALID;
1617 }
1618 if (program->sig_service != NULL((void*)0))
1619 upipe_set_flow_def(program->sig_service, flow_def_dup);
1620
1621 bool_Bool changed = program->sid != sid || program->pmt_pid != pid;
1622 program->sid = sid;
1623 program->pmt_pid = pid;
1624
1625 if (changed)
1626 upipe_notice_va(upipe, "adding program %"PRIu64"l" "u"" on PID %"PRIu64"l" "u",
1627 sid, pid);
1628 else
1629 upipe_notice_va(upipe, "changing program %"PRIu64"l" "u"" on PID %"PRIu64"l" "u",
1630 sid, pid);
1631 return UBASE_ERR_NONE;
1632}

1768/** @internal @This processes control commands on a ts_mux_program pipe.

1773 * @return an error code
1774 */
1775static int upipe_ts_mux_program_control(struct upipe *upipe,
1776 int command, va_list args)
1777{
1778 switch (command) {
1779 case UPIPE_SET_FLOW_DEF: {
1780 struct uref *flow_def = va_arg(args, struct uref *)__builtin_va_arg(args, struct uref *);
1781 return upipe_ts_mux_program_set_flow_def(upipe, flow_def);
1782 }
1783 case UPIPE_GET_SUB_MGR: {
1784 struct upipe_mgr **p = va_arg(args, struct upipe_mgr **)__builtin_va_arg(args, struct upipe_mgr **);
1785 return upipe_ts_mux_program_get_sub_mgr(upipe, p);
1786 }

1788 struct upipe **p = va_arg(args, struct upipe **)__builtin_va_arg(args, struct upipe **);
1789 return upipe_ts_mux_program_iterate_sub(upipe, p);
1790 }

1793 return upipe_ts_mux_program_get_super(upipe, p);

1797 UBASE_SIGNATURE_CHECK(args, UPIPE_TS_MUX_SIGNATURE){ if (__builtin_va_arg(args, unsigned int) != (((uint32_t)'t'

) | (((uint32_t)'x') << 24))) return UBASE_ERR_UNHANDLED
; }

1800 }

1802 UBASE_SIGNATURE_CHECK(args, UPIPE_TS_MUX_SIGNATURE){ if (__builtin_va_arg(args, unsigned int) != (((uint32_t)'t'
) | (((uint32_t)'s') << 8) | (((uint32_t)'m') << 16
) | (((uint32_t)'x') << 24))) return UBASE_ERR_UNHANDLED
; }

1805 }

1807 UBASE_SIGNATURE_CHECK(args, UPIPE_TS_MUX_SIGNATURE){ if (__builtin_va_arg(args, unsigned int) != (((uint32_t)'t'
) | (((uint32_t)'s') << 8) | (((uint32_t)'m') << 16

1837 case UPIPE_TS_MUX_SET_VERSION:

1853

1856 }

1858 return upipe_ts_mux_program_control_bin_input(upipe, command, args);

1861/** @This frees a upipe.
1862 *
1863 * @param urefcount_real pointer to urefcount_real structure
1864 */
1865static void upipe_ts_mux_program_free(struct urefcount *urefcount_real)
1866{
1867 struct upipe_ts_mux_program *upipe_ts_mux_program =
1868 upipe_ts_mux_program_from_urefcount_real(urefcount_real);
1869 struct upipe *upipe = upipe_ts_mux_program_to_upipe(upipe_ts_mux_program);
1870
1871 upipe_throw_dead(upipe);
1872
1873 uprobe_clean(&upipe_ts_mux_program->probe);
1874 urefcount_clean(urefcount_real);
1875 upipe_ts_mux_program_clean_urefcount(upipe);
1876 upipe_ts_mux_program_free_void(upipe);
1877}

1879/** @This is called when there is no external reference to the pipe anymore.
1880 *
1881 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
1882 */
1883static void upipe_ts_mux_program_no_input(struct upipe *upipe)
1884{
1885 struct upipe_ts_mux_program *upipe_ts_mux_program =
1886 upipe_ts_mux_program_from_upipe(upipe);
1887
1888 uref_free(upipe_ts_mux_program->flow_def_input);
1889 upipe_ts_mux_program_clean_bin_input(upipe);

1919/** @internal @This processes control commands.

1922 * @param command type of command to process
1923 * @param args arguments of the command
1924 * @return an error code
1925 */
1926static int upipe_ts_mux_inner_sink_control(struct upipe *sink,
1927 int command, va_list args)

1930 struct upipe *upipe = upipe_ts_mux_to_upipe(upipe_ts_mux);
1931 switch (command) {
1932 case UPIPE_REGISTER_REQUEST: {
1933 struct urequest *request = va_arg(args, struct urequest *)__builtin_va_arg(args, struct urequest *);
1934 return upipe_ts_mux_alloc_output_proxy(upipe, request);
1935 }
1936 case UPIPE_UNREGISTER_REQUEST: {
1937 struct urequest *request = va_arg(args, struct urequest *)__builtin_va_arg(args, struct urequest *);
1938 return upipe_ts_mux_free_output_proxy(upipe, request);
1939 }
1940 case UPIPE_SET_FLOW_DEF:
1941 return UBASE_ERR_NONE;
1942
1943 default:
1944 return UBASE_ERR_UNHANDLED;
1945 }
1946}

2139/** @internal @This increments the cr_sys by a tick, and prepares PSI tables.
2140 *
2141 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
2142 */
2143static void upipe_ts_mux_increment(struct upipe *upipe)
2144{
2145 struct upipe_ts_mux *mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
2146 assert(mux->cr_sys != UINT64_MAX)((mux->cr_sys != (18446744073709551615UL)) ? (void) (0) : __assert_fail
("mux->cr_sys != (18446744073709551615UL)", "upipe_ts_mux.c"
, 2146, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__));
2147 lldiv_t q = lldiv((uint64_t)mux->mtu * UCLOCK_FREQ27000000UL +
2148 mux->cr_sys_remainder, mux->total_octetrate);
2149 mux->cr_sys += q.quot;
2150 mux->cr_sys_remainder = q.rem;
2151
2152 /* Tell PSI tables to prepare packets. */
2153 uint64_t original_cr_sys = mux->cr_sys - mux->latency;
2154 if (mux->psig != NULL((void*)0))
2155 upipe_ts_mux_prepare(mux->psig, original_cr_sys, mux->latency);
2156 if (mux->sig != NULL((void*)0))
2157 upipe_ts_mux_prepare(mux->sig, original_cr_sys, mux->latency);
2158}

2160/** @internal @This shows the next increment of cr_sys.
2161 *
2162 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
2163 * @return the next increment of cr_sys
2164 */
2165static uint64_t upipe_ts_mux_show_increment(struct upipe *upipe)
2166{
2167 struct upipe_ts_mux *mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
2168 assert(mux->cr_sys != UINT64_MAX)((mux->cr_sys != (18446744073709551615UL)) ? (void) (0) : __assert_fail
("mux->cr_sys != (18446744073709551615UL)", "upipe_ts_mux.c"
, 2168, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__));
2169 return mux->cr_sys +
2170 ((uint64_t)mux->mtu * UCLOCK_FREQ27000000UL + mux->cr_sys_remainder) /
2171 mux->total_octetrate;
2172}

2174/** @internal @This splices a ubuf to output.
2175 *
2176 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
2177 * @param ubuf_p filled in with the ubuf to output, or NULL if none is available
2178 * @param dts_sys_p filled with the dts_sys of the fragment
2179 */
2180static void upipe_ts_mux_splice(struct upipe *upipe, struct ubuf **ubuf_p,
2181 uint64_t *dts_sys_p)
2182{
2183 struct upipe_ts_mux *mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
2184 uint64_t original_cr_sys = mux->cr_sys - mux->latency;
2185 struct uchain *uchain;
2186 int err;
2187 *ubuf_p = NULL((void*)0);
2188
2189 /* Order of priority: 1. PSI */
2190 ulist_foreach (&mux->psi_pids, uchain)for ((uchain) = (&mux->psi_pids)->next; (uchain) !=
(&mux->psi_pids); (uchain) = (uchain)->next) {
2191 struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid *psi_pid =
2192 upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_from_uchain(uchain);
2193
2194 if (psi_pid->dts_sys < original_cr_sys) /* flush */
2195 upipe_ts_encaps_splice(psi_pid->encaps, original_cr_sys,
2196 NULL((void*)0), NULL((void*)0));
2197
2198 if (psi_pid->cr_sys <= original_cr_sys) {
2199 err = upipe_ts_encaps_splice(psi_pid->encaps, original_cr_sys,
2200 ubuf_p, dts_sys_p);
2201 if (!ubase_check(err)) {
2202 upipe_warn(upipe, "internal error in splice")uprobe_log((upipe)->uprobe, upipe, UPROBE_LOG_WARNING, "internal error in splice"
);
2203 upipe_throw_fatal(upipe, err)do { uprobe_err_va((upipe)->uprobe, upipe, "fatal error at %s:%d (0x%x)"
, "upipe_ts_mux.c", 2203, err); uprobe_throw((upipe)->uprobe
, upipe, UPROBE_FATAL, err); } while (0);
2204 }
2205 return;
2206 }
2207 }
2208
2209 /* 2. Inputs */
2210 uint64_t cr_sys = UINT64_MAX(18446744073709551615UL);
2211 struct upipe_ts_mux_input *selected_input = NULL((void*)0);
2212 ulist_foreach (&mux->programs, uchain)for ((uchain) = (&mux->programs)->next; (uchain) !=
(&mux->programs); (uchain) = (uchain)->next) {
2213 struct upipe_ts_mux_program *program =
2214 upipe_ts_mux_program_from_uchain(uchain);
2215 struct uchain *uchain_input;
2216 ulist_foreach (&program->inputs, uchain_input)for ((uchain_input) = (&program->inputs)->next; (uchain_input
) != (&program->inputs); (uchain_input) = (uchain_input
)->next) {
2217 struct upipe_ts_mux_input *input =
2218 upipe_ts_mux_input_from_uchain(uchain_input);
2219 if (input->dts_sys < original_cr_sys) /* flush */
2220 upipe_ts_encaps_splice(input->encaps, original_cr_sys,
2221 NULL((void*)0), NULL((void*)0));
2222
2223 if (input->dts_sys <= original_cr_sys + mux->interval ||
2224 input->pcr_sys <= original_cr_sys) {
2225 selected_input = input;
2226 goto upipe_ts_mux_splice_done;
2227 }
2228 if (input->cr_sys < cr_sys) {
2229 selected_input = input;
2230 cr_sys = input->cr_sys;
2231 }
2232 }
2233 }
2234
2235 if (selected_input == NULL((void*)0) || selected_input->cr_sys > original_cr_sys)
2236 return;
2237
2238upipe_ts_mux_splice_done:
2239 err = upipe_ts_encaps_splice(selected_input->encaps, original_cr_sys,
2240 ubuf_p, dts_sys_p);
2241 if (!ubase_check(err)) {
2242 upipe_warn(upipe, "internal error in splice")uprobe_log((upipe)->uprobe, upipe, UPROBE_LOG_WARNING, "internal error in splice"
);
2243 upipe_throw_fatal(upipe, err)do { uprobe_err_va((upipe)->uprobe, upipe, "fatal error at %s:%d (0x%x)"
, "upipe_ts_mux.c", 2243, err); uprobe_throw((upipe)->uprobe
, upipe, UPROBE_FATAL, err); } while (0);
2244 }
2245
2246 if (selected_input->deleted && !selected_input->ready) {
2247 /* This triggers the immediate deletion of the input. */
2248 upipe_release(selected_input->encaps);
2249 }
2250}

2252/** @internal @This appends a uref to our buffer.
2253 *
2254 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
2255 * @param ubuf ubuf to append
2256 * @param dts_sys dts_sys associated with the ubuf
2257 */
2258static void upipe_ts_mux_append(struct upipe *upipe, struct ubuf *ubuf,
2259 uint64_t dts_sys)
2260{
2261 struct upipe_ts_mux *mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
2262 if (mux->uref == NULL((void*)0)) {
2263 mux->uref = uref_alloc(mux->uref_mgr);
2264 if (unlikely(mux->uref == NULL)__builtin_expect(!!(mux->uref == ((void*)0)),0)) {
2265 upipe_throw_fatal(upipe, UBASE_ERR_ALLOC)do { uprobe_err_va((upipe)->uprobe, upipe, "fatal error at %s:%d (0x%x)"
, "upipe_ts_mux.c", 2265, UBASE_ERR_ALLOC); uprobe_throw((upipe
)->uprobe, upipe, UPROBE_FATAL, UBASE_ERR_ALLOC); } while (
0);
2266 ubuf_free(ubuf);
2267 return;
2268 }
2269 uref_clock_set_cr_sys(mux->uref, mux->cr_sys - mux->latency);
2270 if (dts_sys != UINT64_MAX(18446744073709551615UL))
2271 uref_clock_set_cr_dts_delay(mux->uref,
2272 dts_sys - (mux->cr_sys - mux->latency));
2273 uref_attach_ubuf(mux->uref, ubuf);
2274 } else {
2275 uint64_t current_dts_sys;
2276 if (dts_sys != UINT64_MAX(18446744073709551615UL) &&
2277 (!ubase_check(uref_clock_get_dts_sys(mux->uref,
2278 &current_dts_sys)) ||
2279 current_dts_sys > dts_sys))
2280 uref_clock_set_cr_dts_delay(mux->uref,
2281 dts_sys - (mux->cr_sys - mux->latency));
2282 uref_block_append(mux->uref, ubuf);
2283 }
2284 mux->uref_size += TS_SIZE188;
2285}

2295 struct uref *uref = mux->uref;

2297 mux->uref_size = 0;
2298 upipe_ts_mux_output(upipe, uref, upump_p);

2300
2301/** @internal @This runs when the pump expires (live mode only).
2302 *
2303 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
2304 */
2305static void _upipe_ts_mux_watcher(struct upipe *upipe)
2306{
2307 upipe_use(upipe);
2308 struct upipe_ts_mux *mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
2309 if (unlikely(mux->cr_sys == UINT64_MAX)__builtin_expect(!!(mux->cr_sys == (18446744073709551615UL
)),0))
2310 mux->cr_sys = uclock_now(mux->uclock);
2311
2312 upipe_ts_mux_increment(upipe);
2313 if (mux->uref != NULL((void*)0)) /* capped VBR */
2314 uref_clock_set_cr_sys(mux->uref, mux->cr_sys - mux->latency);
2315
2316 while (mux->uref_size < mux->mtu) {
2317 struct ubuf *ubuf;
2318 uint64_t dts_sys;
2319 upipe_ts_mux_splice(upipe, &ubuf, &dts_sys);
2320 if (ubuf == NULL((void*)0))
2321 break;
2322 upipe_ts_mux_append(upipe, ubuf, dts_sys);
2323 }
2324
2325 uint64_t dts_sys;
2326 if (mux->mode != UPIPE_TS_MUX_MODE_CAPPED ||
2327 (mux->uref != NULL((void*)0) &&
2328 ubase_check(uref_clock_get_dts_sys(mux->uref, &dts_sys)) &&
2329 dts_sys + mux->latency < upipe_ts_mux_show_increment(upipe))) {
2330 while (mux->uref_size < mux->mtu) {
2331 struct ubuf *ubuf = ubuf_dup(mux->padding);
2332 if (ubuf == NULL((void*)0))
2333 break;
2334 upipe_ts_mux_append(upipe, ubuf, UINT64_MAX(18446744073709551615UL));
2335 }
2336 }
2337
2338 if (mux->uref_size >= mux->mtu)
2339 upipe_ts_mux_complete(upipe, &mux->upump);
2340
2341 /* Check for deleted inputs */
2342 struct uchain *uchain_program, *uchain_program_tmp;
2343 ulist_delete_foreach (&mux->programs, uchain_program, uchain_program_tmp)for ((uchain_program) = (&mux->programs)->next, (uchain_program_tmp
) = (uchain_program)->next; (uchain_program) != (&mux->
programs); (uchain_program) = (uchain_program_tmp), (uchain_program_tmp
) = (uchain_program)->next) {

2346 upipe_use(upipe_ts_mux_program_to_upipe(program));
2347

2349 ulist_delete_foreach (&program->inputs, uchain_input,for ((uchain_input) = (&program->inputs)->next, (uchain_input_tmp

2355 }
2356 upipe_release(upipe_ts_mux_program_to_upipe(program));
2357 }

2374/** @internal @This checks whether a packet is available on all inputs
2375 * (used in a file mode only).
2376 *
2377 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
2378 * @return the lowest available date, or UINT64_MAX
2379 */
2380static uint64_t upipe_ts_mux_check_available(struct upipe *upipe)
2381{
2382 struct upipe_ts_mux *mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
2383 uint64_t min_cr_sys = UINT64_MAX(18446744073709551615UL);
2384
2385 struct uchain *uchain_program, *uchain_program_tmp;
2386 ulist_delete_foreach (&mux->programs, uchain_program,for ((uchain_program) = (&mux->programs)->next, (uchain_program_tmp
) = (uchain_program)->next; (uchain_program) != (&mux->
programs); (uchain_program) = (uchain_program_tmp), (uchain_program_tmp
) = (uchain_program)->next)
2387 uchain_program_tmp)for ((uchain_program) = (&mux->programs)->next, (uchain_program_tmp
) = (uchain_program)->next; (uchain_program) != (&mux->
programs); (uchain_program) = (uchain_program_tmp), (uchain_program_tmp
) = (uchain_program)->next) {
2388 struct upipe_ts_mux_program *program =
2389 upipe_ts_mux_program_from_uchain(uchain_program);
2390 upipe_use(upipe_ts_mux_program_to_upipe(program));
2391
2392 struct uchain *uchain_input, *uchain_input_tmp;
2393 ulist_delete_foreach (&program->inputs, uchain_input,for ((uchain_input) = (&program->inputs)->next, (uchain_input_tmp
) = (uchain_input)->next; (uchain_input) != (&program->
inputs); (uchain_input) = (uchain_input_tmp), (uchain_input_tmp
) = (uchain_input)->next)
2394 uchain_input_tmp)for ((uchain_input) = (&program->inputs)->next, (uchain_input_tmp
) = (uchain_input)->next; (uchain_input) != (&program->
inputs); (uchain_input) = (uchain_input_tmp), (uchain_input_tmp
) = (uchain_input)->next) {
2395 struct upipe_ts_mux_input *input =
2396 upipe_ts_mux_input_from_uchain(uchain_input);
2397 if (!input->ready) {
2398 if (input->deleted) {
2399 upipe_release(input->encaps);
2400 continue;
2401 } else if (input->input_type != UPIPE_TS_MUX_INPUT_OTHER) {
2402 upipe_release(upipe_ts_mux_program_to_upipe(program));
2403 return UINT64_MAX(18446744073709551615UL);
2404 }
2405 }
2406 if (min_cr_sys > input->cr_sys)
2407 min_cr_sys = input->cr_sys;
2408 }
2409 upipe_release(upipe_ts_mux_program_to_upipe(program));
2410 }
2411 return min_cr_sys;
2412}

2431/** @internal @This checks if a packet must be output in file mode.
2432 *
2433 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
2434 * @param upump_p reference to pump that generated the buffer
2435 */
2436static void upipe_ts_mux_work_file(struct upipe *upipe, struct upump **upump_p)
2437{
2438 struct upipe_ts_mux *mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
2439 uint64_t min_cr_sys;
2440#ifdef DEBUG_FILE
2441 upipe_verbose(upipe, "work file starting")uprobe_log((upipe)->uprobe, upipe, UPROBE_LOG_VERBOSE, "work file starting"
);
2442#endif
2443 while ((min_cr_sys = upipe_ts_mux_check_available(upipe)) !=
2444 UINT64_MAX(18446744073709551615UL)) {
2445#ifdef DEBUG_FILE
2446 upipe_verbose(upipe, "work file running")uprobe_log((upipe)->uprobe, upipe, UPROBE_LOG_VERBOSE, "work file running"
);
2447#endif
2448 if (mux->cr_sys == UINT64_MAX(18446744073709551615UL)) {
2449 upipe_verbose_va(upipe, "work file min=%"PRIu64"l" "u", min_cr_sys);
2450 mux->cr_sys = min_cr_sys + mux->latency;
2451 if (mux->initial_cr_prog != UINT64_MAX(18446744073709551615UL)) {
2452 upipe_ts_mux_init_cr_prog(upipe, mux->initial_cr_prog);
2453 mux->initial_cr_prog = UINT64_MAX(18446744073709551615UL);
2454 }
2455 upipe_ts_mux_prepare(mux->psig, min_cr_sys, 0);
2456 if (mux->sig != NULL((void*)0))
2457 upipe_ts_mux_prepare(mux->sig, min_cr_sys, 0);
2458 }
2459
2460 struct ubuf *ubuf;
2461 uint64_t dts_sys;
2462 upipe_ts_mux_splice(upipe, &ubuf, &dts_sys);
2463 if (ubuf != NULL((void*)0)) {
2464 upipe_ts_mux_append(upipe, ubuf, dts_sys);
2465 if (mux->uref_size >= mux->mtu) {
2466 upipe_ts_mux_complete(upipe, &mux->upump);
2467 upipe_ts_mux_increment(upipe);
2468 }
2469 continue;
2470 }
2471
2472 if (mux->mode == UPIPE_TS_MUX_MODE_CAPPED &&
2473 (mux->uref == NULL((void*)0) ||
2474 !ubase_check(uref_clock_get_dts_sys(mux->uref, &dts_sys)) ||
2475 dts_sys + mux->latency >= upipe_ts_mux_show_increment(upipe))) {
2476 upipe_ts_mux_increment(upipe);
2477 continue;
2478 }
2479
2480 while (mux->uref_size < mux->mtu) {
2481 struct ubuf *ubuf = ubuf_dup(mux->padding);
2482 if (ubuf == NULL((void*)0))
2483 break;
2484 upipe_ts_mux_append(upipe, ubuf, UINT64_MAX(18446744073709551615UL));
2485 }
2486
2487 upipe_ts_mux_complete(upipe, upump_p);
2488 upipe_ts_mux_increment(upipe);
2489 }
2490#ifdef DEBUG_FILE
2491 upipe_verbose(upipe, "work file leaving")uprobe_log((upipe)->uprobe, upipe, UPROBE_LOG_VERBOSE, "work file leaving"
);
2492#endif
2493}

2495/** @internal @This checks if a packet must be output in live mode.
2496 *
2497 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
2498 * @param upump_p reference to pump that generated the buffer
2499 */
2500static void upipe_ts_mux_work_live(struct upipe *upipe, struct upump **upump_p)
2501{
2502 struct upipe_ts_mux *mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
2503 if (likely(mux->upump != NULL)__builtin_expect(!!(mux->upump != ((void*)0)),1))
2504 return;
2505
2506 upipe_ts_mux_check_upump_mgr(upipe);
2507 if (mux->upump_mgr == NULL((void*)0))
2508 return;
2509
2510 struct upump *upump = NULL((void*)0);
2511 if (likely(mux->cr_sys != UINT64_MAX)__builtin_expect(!!(mux->cr_sys != (18446744073709551615UL
)),1)) {
2512 uint64_t next_cr_sys = upipe_ts_mux_show_increment(upipe);
2513 uint64_t now = uclock_now(mux->uclock);
2514 if (next_cr_sys > now + mux->mux_delay) {
2515 upump = upump_alloc_timer(mux->upump_mgr, upipe_ts_mux_watcher,
2516 upipe, next_cr_sys - now - mux->mux_delay,
2517 0);
2518 if (unlikely(upump == NULL)__builtin_expect(!!(upump == ((void*)0)),0)) {
2519 upipe_throw_fatal(upipe, UBASE_ERR_UPUMP)do { uprobe_err_va((upipe)->uprobe, upipe, "fatal error at %s:%d (0x%x)"
, "upipe_ts_mux.c", 2519, UBASE_ERR_UPUMP); uprobe_throw((upipe
)->uprobe, upipe, UPROBE_FATAL, UBASE_ERR_UPUMP); } while (
0);
2520 return;
2521 }
2522 } else if (next_cr_sys > now) {
2523 _upipe_ts_mux_watcher(upipe);
2524 return;
2525 } else
2526 upipe_warn_va(upipe, "missed a tick by %"PRIu64"l" "u"" ms",
2527 (now - next_cr_sys) * 1000 / UCLOCK_FREQ27000000UL);
2528 }
2529 if (unlikely(upump == NULL)__builtin_expect(!!(upump == ((void*)0)),0)) {
2530 mux->cr_sys = UINT64_MAX(18446744073709551615UL);
2531 mux->cr_sys_remainder = 0;
2532 upump = upump_alloc_idler(mux->upump_mgr, upipe_ts_mux_watcher, upipe);
2533 if (unlikely(upump == NULL)__builtin_expect(!!(upump == ((void*)0)),0)) {
2534 upipe_throw_fatal(upipe, UBASE_ERR_UPUMP)do { uprobe_err_va((upipe)->uprobe, upipe, "fatal error at %s:%d (0x%x)"
, "upipe_ts_mux.c", 2534, UBASE_ERR_UPUMP); uprobe_throw((upipe
)->uprobe, upipe, UPROBE_FATAL, UBASE_ERR_UPUMP); } while (
0);
2535 return;
2536 }
2537 }
2538 upump_start(upump);
2539 upipe_ts_mux_set_upump(upipe, upump);
2540}

2542/** @internal @This checks if a packet must be output.
2543 *
2544 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
2545 * @param upump_p reference to pump that generated the buffer
2546 */
2547static void upipe_ts_mux_work(struct upipe *upipe, struct upump **upump_p)
2548{
2549 struct upipe_ts_mux *mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
2550 if (unlikely(mux->flow_def == NULL || mux->padding == NULL ||__builtin_expect(!!(mux->flow_def == ((void*)0) || mux->

2551 !mux->interval)__builtin_expect(!!(mux->flow_def == ((void*)0) || mux->
padding == ((void*)0) || !mux->interval),0))
2552 return;
2553
2554 if (urequest_get_opaque(&mux->uclock_request, struct upipe *)(struct upipe *)(&mux->uclock_request)->opaque == NULL((void*)0))
2555 upipe_ts_mux_work_file(upipe, upump_p);
2556 else
2557 upipe_ts_mux_work_live(upipe, upump_p);
2558}

2643/** @This prints the current operating mode of the mux.
2644 *
2645 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
2646 */
2647static void upipe_ts_mux_notice(struct upipe *upipe)
2648{
2649 struct upipe_ts_mux *mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
2650 if (mux->uclock != NULL((void*)0)) {
2651 if (mux->total_octetrate == mux->required_octetrate)
2652 upipe_notice_va(upipe,
2653 "now operating in %s mode at %"PRIu64"l" "u"" bits/s (auto), conformance %s, latency %"PRIu64"l" "u"" ms",
2654 upipe_ts_mux_mode_print(mux->mode),
2655 mux->total_octetrate * 8,
2656 upipe_ts_conformance_print(mux->conformance),
2657 (mux->latency + mux->mux_delay) * 1000 / UCLOCK_FREQ27000000UL);
2658 else
2659 upipe_notice_va(upipe,
2660 "now operating in %s mode at %"PRIu64"l" "u"" bits/s (requires %"PRIu64"l" "u"" bits/s), conformance %s, latency %"PRIu64"l" "u"" ms",
2661 upipe_ts_mux_mode_print(mux->mode),
2662 mux->total_octetrate * 8, mux->required_octetrate * 8,
2663 upipe_ts_conformance_print(mux->conformance),
2664 (mux->latency + mux->mux_delay) * 1000 / UCLOCK_FREQ27000000UL);
2665 } else {
2666 if (mux->total_octetrate == mux->required_octetrate)
2667 upipe_notice_va(upipe,
2668 "now operating in %s mode at %"PRIu64"l" "u"" bits/s (auto), conformance %s",
2669 upipe_ts_mux_mode_print(mux->mode),
2670 mux->total_octetrate * 8,
2671 upipe_ts_conformance_print(mux->conformance));
2672 else
2673 upipe_notice_va(upipe,
2674 "now operating in %s mode at %"PRIu64"l" "u"" bits/s (requires %"PRIu64"l" "u"" bits/s), conformance %s",
2675 upipe_ts_mux_mode_print(mux->mode),
2676 mux->total_octetrate * 8, mux->required_octetrate * 8,
2677 upipe_ts_conformance_print(mux->conformance));
2678 }
2679}
2680
2681/** @This calculates the total octetrate used by a stream and updates the
2682 * mux.
2683 *
2684 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
2685 */
2686static void upipe_ts_mux_update(struct upipe *upipe)
2687{
2688 struct upipe_ts_mux *mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
2689 uint64_t required_octetrate = mux->padding_octetrate;
2690 struct uchain *uchain;
2691 ulist_foreach (&mux->psi_pids, uchain)for ((uchain) = (&mux->psi_pids)->next; (uchain) !=
(&mux->psi_pids); (uchain) = (uchain)->next) {
2692 struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid *psi_pid =
2693 upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_from_uchain(uchain);
2694 required_octetrate += psi_pid->octetrate;
2695 }
2696
2697 ulist_foreach (&mux->programs, uchain)for ((uchain) = (&mux->programs)->next; (uchain) !=
(&mux->programs); (uchain) = (uchain)->next) {
2698 struct upipe_ts_mux_program *program =
2699 upipe_ts_mux_program_from_uchain(uchain);
2700 required_octetrate += program->required_octetrate;
2701 }
2702
2703 /* Add a margin to take into account 1/ the drift of the input clock
2704 * 2/ the drift of the output clock. */
2705 required_octetrate +=
2706 (required_octetrate * PCR_TOLERANCE_PPM30 * 2 + 999999) / 1000000;
2707 mux->required_octetrate = required_octetrate;
2708
2709 uint64_t total_octetrate = mux->fixed_octetrate;
2710 if (!total_octetrate)
2711 total_octetrate = required_octetrate;
2712
2713 if (total_octetrate != mux->total_octetrate) {
2714 mux->total_octetrate = total_octetrate;
2715 upipe_ts_mux_build_flow_def(upipe);
2716 upipe_ts_mux_set_upump(upipe, NULL((void*)0));
2717 }
2718
2719 if (mux->total_octetrate) {
2720 mux->interval = (mux->mtu * UCLOCK_FREQ27000000UL + mux->total_octetrate - 1) /
2721 mux->total_octetrate;
2722 upipe_ts_mux_set_pat_interval(mux->psig,
2723 mux->interval < mux->pat_interval / 2 ?
2724 mux->pat_interval - (mux->pat_interval % mux->interval) :
2725 mux->pat_interval);
2726
2727 if (mux->sig != NULL((void*)0)) {
2728 upipe_ts_mux_set_nit_interval(mux->sig,
2729 mux->interval < mux->nit_interval / 2 ?
2730 mux->nit_interval - (mux->nit_interval % mux->interval) :
2731 mux->nit_interval);
2732 upipe_ts_mux_set_sdt_interval(mux->sig,
2733 mux->interval < mux->sdt_interval / 2 ?
2734 mux->sdt_interval - (mux->sdt_interval % mux->interval) :
2735 mux->sdt_interval);
2736 if (mux->uclock != NULL((void*)0))
2737 upipe_ts_mux_set_tdt_interval(mux->sig,
2738 mux->interval < mux->tdt_interval / 2 ?
2739 mux->tdt_interval - (mux->tdt_interval % mux->interval) :
2740 mux->tdt_interval);
2741 }
2742
2743 struct uchain *uchain_program;
2744 ulist_foreach (&mux->programs, uchain_program)for ((uchain_program) = (&mux->programs)->next; (uchain_program
) != (&mux->programs); (uchain_program) = (uchain_program
)->next) {
2745 struct upipe_ts_mux_program *program =
2746 upipe_ts_mux_program_from_uchain(uchain_program);
2747 upipe_ts_mux_set_pmt_interval(program->psig_program,
2748 mux->interval < program->pmt_interval / 2 ?
2749 program->pmt_interval -
2750 (program->pmt_interval % mux->interval) :
2751 program->pmt_interval);
2752
2753 if (program->sig_service != NULL((void*)0)) {
2754 upipe_ts_mux_set_eit_interval(program->sig_service,
2755 mux->interval < program->eit_interval / 2 ?
2756 program->eit_interval -
2757 (program->eit_interval % mux->interval) :
2758 program->eit_interval);
2759 }
2760
2761 struct uchain *uchain_input;
2762 ulist_foreach (&program->inputs, uchain_input)for ((uchain_input) = (&program->inputs)->next; (uchain_input
) != (&program->inputs); (uchain_input) = (uchain_input
)->next) {
2763 struct upipe_ts_mux_input *input =
2764 upipe_ts_mux_input_from_uchain(uchain_input);
2765 if (input->pcr && input->encaps != NULL((void*)0))
2766 upipe_ts_mux_set_pcr_interval(input->encaps,
2767 mux->interval < program->pcr_interval / 2 ?
2768 program->pcr_interval -
2769 (program->pcr_interval % mux->interval) :
2770 program->pcr_interval);
2771 }
2772 }
2773 }
2774
2775 upipe_ts_mux_notice(upipe);
2776}
2777
2778/** @internal @This builds the output flow definition.
2779 *
2780 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
2781 */
2782static void upipe_ts_mux_build_flow_def(struct upipe *upipe)
2783{
2784 struct upipe_ts_mux *mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
2785 if (mux->uref_mgr == NULL((void*)0))
2786 return;
2787
2788 struct uref *flow_def =
2789 uref_block_flow_alloc_def(mux->uref_mgr, "mpegtsaligned.");
2790 if (unlikely(flow_def == NULL)__builtin_expect(!!(flow_def == ((void*)0)),0)) {
2791 upipe_throw_fatal(upipe, UBASE_ERR_ALLOC)do { uprobe_err_va((upipe)->uprobe, upipe, "fatal error at %s:%d (0x%x)"
, "upipe_ts_mux.c", 2791, UBASE_ERR_ALLOC); uprobe_throw((upipe
)->uprobe, upipe, UPROBE_FATAL, UBASE_ERR_ALLOC); } while (
0);
2792 return;
2793 }
2794
2795 if (unlikely(!ubase_check(uref_clock_set_latency(flow_def,__builtin_expect(!!(!ubase_check(uref_clock_set_latency(flow_def
, mux->latency + mux->mux_delay)) || !ubase_check(uref_block_flow_set_octetrate
(flow_def, mux->total_octetrate)) || !ubase_check(uref_block_flow_set_size
(flow_def, mux->mtu))),0)
2796 mux->latency + mux->mux_delay)) ||__builtin_expect(!!(!ubase_check(uref_clock_set_latency(flow_def
, mux->latency + mux->mux_delay)) || !ubase_check(uref_block_flow_set_octetrate
(flow_def, mux->total_octetrate)) || !ubase_check(uref_block_flow_set_size
(flow_def, mux->mtu))),0)
2797 !ubase_check(uref_block_flow_set_octetrate(flow_def,__builtin_expect(!!(!ubase_check(uref_clock_set_latency(flow_def
, mux->latency + mux->mux_delay)) || !ubase_check(uref_block_flow_set_octetrate
(flow_def, mux->total_octetrate)) || !ubase_check(uref_block_flow_set_size
(flow_def, mux->mtu))),0)
2798 mux->total_octetrate)) ||__builtin_expect(!!(!ubase_check(uref_clock_set_latency(flow_def
, mux->latency + mux->mux_delay)) || !ubase_check(uref_block_flow_set_octetrate
(flow_def, mux->total_octetrate)) || !ubase_check(uref_block_flow_set_size
(flow_def, mux->mtu))),0)
2799 !ubase_check(uref_block_flow_set_size(flow_def,__builtin_expect(!!(!ubase_check(uref_clock_set_latency(flow_def
, mux->latency + mux->mux_delay)) || !ubase_check(uref_block_flow_set_octetrate
(flow_def, mux->total_octetrate)) || !ubase_check(uref_block_flow_set_size
(flow_def, mux->mtu))),0)
2800 mux->mtu)))__builtin_expect(!!(!ubase_check(uref_clock_set_latency(flow_def
, mux->latency + mux->mux_delay)) || !ubase_check(uref_block_flow_set_octetrate
(flow_def, mux->total_octetrate)) || !ubase_check(uref_block_flow_set_size
(flow_def, mux->mtu))),0))
2801 upipe_throw_fatal(upipe, UBASE_ERR_ALLOC)do { uprobe_err_va((upipe)->uprobe, upipe, "fatal error at %s:%d (0x%x)"
, "upipe_ts_mux.c", 2801, UBASE_ERR_ALLOC); uprobe_throw((upipe
)->uprobe, upipe, UPROBE_FATAL, UBASE_ERR_ALLOC); } while (
0);
2802 upipe_ts_mux_store_flow_def(upipe, flow_def);
2803
2804
2805 struct uchain *uchain_program;
2806 ulist_foreach (&mux->programs, uchain_program)for ((uchain_program) = (&mux->programs)->next; (uchain_program
) != (&mux->programs); (uchain_program) = (uchain_program
)->next) {
2807 struct upipe_ts_mux_program *program =
2808 upipe_ts_mux_program_from_uchain(uchain_program);
2809 struct uchain *uchain_input;
2810 ulist_foreach (&program->inputs, uchain_input)for ((uchain_input) = (&program->inputs)->next; (uchain_input
) != (&program->inputs); (uchain_input) = (uchain_input
)->next) {
2811 struct upipe_ts_mux_input *input =
2812 upipe_ts_mux_input_from_uchain(uchain_input);
2813 if (input->encaps != NULL((void*)0) && input->original_au_per_sec.den)
2814 upipe_set_max_length(input->encaps,
2815 (MIN_BUFFERING(27000000UL * 10) + mux->latency) *
2816 input->original_au_per_sec.num /
2817 input->original_au_per_sec.den / UCLOCK_FREQ27000000UL);
2818 }
2819 }
2820}

2822/** @internal @This builds an appropriate flow definition packet, and
2823 * sends it to generators.
2824 *
2825 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
2826 */
2827static void upipe_ts_mux_conformance_flow_def(struct upipe *upipe)
2828{
2829 struct upipe_ts_mux *upipe_ts_mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
2830 if (upipe_ts_mux->flow_def_input == NULL((void*)0))
2831 return;
2832
2833 if (upipe_ts_conformance_from_flow_def(upipe_ts_mux->flow_def_input) ==
2834 upipe_ts_mux->conformance) {
2835 upipe_set_flow_def(upipe_ts_mux->psig, upipe_ts_mux->flow_def_input);
2836 if (upipe_ts_mux->sig != NULL((void*)0))
2837 upipe_set_flow_def(upipe_ts_mux->sig, upipe_ts_mux->flow_def_input);
2838 return;
2839 }
2840
2841 struct uref *flow_def_dup;
2842 if (unlikely((flow_def_dup = uref_dup(upipe_ts_mux->flow_def_input)) ==__builtin_expect(!!((flow_def_dup = uref_dup(upipe_ts_mux->
flow_def_input)) == ((void*)0) || !ubase_check(upipe_ts_conformance_to_flow_def
(flow_def_dup, upipe_ts_mux->conformance))),0)
2843 NULL ||__builtin_expect(!!((flow_def_dup = uref_dup(upipe_ts_mux->
flow_def_input)) == ((void*)0) || !ubase_check(upipe_ts_conformance_to_flow_def
(flow_def_dup, upipe_ts_mux->conformance))),0)
2844 !ubase_check(upipe_ts_conformance_to_flow_def(flow_def_dup,__builtin_expect(!!((flow_def_dup = uref_dup(upipe_ts_mux->
flow_def_input)) == ((void*)0) || !ubase_check(upipe_ts_conformance_to_flow_def
(flow_def_dup, upipe_ts_mux->conformance))),0)
2845 upipe_ts_mux->conformance)))__builtin_expect(!!((flow_def_dup = uref_dup(upipe_ts_mux->
flow_def_input)) == ((void*)0) || !ubase_check(upipe_ts_conformance_to_flow_def
(flow_def_dup, upipe_ts_mux->conformance))),0)) {
2846 uref_free(flow_def_dup);
2847 upipe_throw_fatal(upipe, UBASE_ERR_ALLOC)do { uprobe_err_va((upipe)->uprobe, upipe, "fatal error at %s:%d (0x%x)"
, "upipe_ts_mux.c", 2847, UBASE_ERR_ALLOC); uprobe_throw((upipe
)->uprobe, upipe, UPROBE_FATAL, UBASE_ERR_ALLOC); } while (
0);
2848 return;
2849 }
2850
2851 upipe_set_flow_def(upipe_ts_mux->psig, flow_def_dup);
2852 if (upipe_ts_mux->sig != NULL((void*)0))
2853 upipe_set_flow_def(upipe_ts_mux->sig, flow_def_dup);
2854 uref_free(flow_def_dup);
2855}
2856
2857/** @internal @This updates the PSI generator.
2858 *
2859 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
2860 */
2861static void upipe_ts_mux_update_psig(struct upipe *upipe)
2862{
2863 struct upipe_ts_mux *upipe_ts_mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
2864 /* Fix up PSI and PCR intervals */
2865 uint64_t max_psi_interval = UINT64_MAX(18446744073709551615UL);
2866 uint64_t max_pcr_interval = MAX_PCR_INTERVAL_ISO(27000000UL / 10);
2867 switch (upipe_ts_mux->conformance) {
2868 case UPIPE_TS_CONFORMANCE_DVB:
2869 case UPIPE_TS_CONFORMANCE_DVB_NO_TABLES:
2870 case UPIPE_TS_CONFORMANCE_ISDB:
2871 max_psi_interval = MAX_PSI_INTERVAL_DVB(27000000UL / 10);
2872 max_pcr_interval = MAX_PCR_INTERVAL_DVB(27000000UL / 25);
2873 break;
2874 case UPIPE_TS_CONFORMANCE_ATSC:
2875 max_psi_interval = MAX_PSI_INTERVAL_ATSC(27000000UL / 10);
2876 break;
2877 default:
2878 break;
2879 }
2880
2881 if (upipe_ts_mux->pat_interval > max_psi_interval)
2882 upipe_ts_mux->pat_interval = max_psi_interval;
2883 if (upipe_ts_mux->pmt_interval > max_psi_interval)
2884 upipe_ts_mux->pmt_interval = max_psi_interval;
2885 if (upipe_ts_mux->pcr_interval > max_pcr_interval)
2886 upipe_ts_mux->pcr_interval = max_pcr_interval;
2887
2888 struct uchain *uchain;
2889 ulist_foreach (&upipe_ts_mux->programs, uchain)for ((uchain) = (&upipe_ts_mux->programs)->next; (uchain
) != (&upipe_ts_mux->programs); (uchain) = (uchain)->
next) {
2890 struct upipe_ts_mux_program *program =
2891 upipe_ts_mux_program_from_uchain(uchain);
2892 if (program->pmt_interval > max_psi_interval)
2893 program->pmt_interval = max_psi_interval;
2894 if (program->pcr_interval > max_pcr_interval)
2895 program->pcr_interval = max_pcr_interval;
2896 }
2897}
2898
2899/** @internal @This updates the SI generator.
2900 *
2901 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
2902 */
2903static void upipe_ts_mux_update_sig(struct upipe *upipe)
2904{
2905 struct upipe_ts_mux *mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
2906 if (mux->conformance != UPIPE_TS_CONFORMANCE_DVB &&
2907 mux->conformance != UPIPE_TS_CONFORMANCE_ISDB) {
2908 if (mux->sig == NULL((void*)0))
2909 return;
2910
2911 upipe_release(mux->psig_nit);
2912 mux->psig_nit = NULL((void*)0);
2913 upipe_release(mux->sig);
2914 mux->sig = NULL((void*)0);
2915 upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_release(mux->psi_pid_nit);
2916 mux->psi_pid_nit = NULL((void*)0);
2917 upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_release(mux->psi_pid_sdt);
2918 mux->psi_pid_sdt = NULL((void*)0);

2923

) || mux->psi_pid_tdt == ((void*)0) || (mux->sig = upipe_ts_sig_alloc

3007/** @internal @This changes the current conformance, and starts necessary
3008 * generators.
3009 *
3010 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
3011 * @param conformance conformance mode
3012 */
3013static void upipe_ts_mux_conformance_change(struct upipe *upipe,
3014 enum upipe_ts_conformance conformance)
3015{
3016 struct upipe_ts_mux *upipe_ts_mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
3017 if (upipe_ts_mux->conformance == conformance)
3018 return;
3019
3020 upipe_ts_mux->conformance = conformance;
3021
3022 upipe_ts_mux_update_psig(upipe);
3023 upipe_ts_mux_update_sig(upipe);
3024 upipe_ts_mux_update(upipe);
3025 upipe_ts_mux_conformance_flow_def(upipe);
3026}
3027
3028/** @internal @This tries to guess the conformance of the stream from the
3029 * information that is available to us.
3030 *
3031 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
3032 */
3033static void upipe_ts_mux_conformance_guess(struct upipe *upipe)
3034{
3035 struct upipe_ts_mux *upipe_ts_mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
3036 if (!upipe_ts_mux->auto_conformance)
3037 return;
3038 if (upipe_ts_mux->flow_def_input == NULL((void*)0))
3039 upipe_ts_mux_conformance_change(upipe,
3040 UPIPE_TS_CONFORMANCE_DVB_NO_TABLES);
3041 else
3042 upipe_ts_mux_conformance_change(upipe,
3043 upipe_ts_conformance_from_flow_def(upipe_ts_mux->flow_def_input));
3044}
3045
3046/** @internal @This sets the input flow definition.
3047 *
3048 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
3049 * @param flow_def flow definition packet
3050 * @return an error code
3051 */
3052static int upipe_ts_mux_set_flow_def(struct upipe *upipe, struct uref *flow_def)
3053{
3054 if (flow_def == NULL((void*)0))
3055 return UBASE_ERR_INVALID;
3056
3057 struct upipe_ts_mux *upipe_ts_mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
3058 UBASE_RETURN(uref_flow_match_def(flow_def, "void."))do { int ubase_err_tmp = uref_flow_match_def(flow_def, "void."
); if (__builtin_expect(!!(!ubase_check(ubase_err_tmp)),0)) return
ubase_err_tmp; } while (0);
3059 struct uref *flow_def_dup;
3060 if (unlikely((flow_def_dup = uref_dup(flow_def)) == NULL)__builtin_expect(!!((flow_def_dup = uref_dup(flow_def)) == ((
void*)0)),0))
3061 return UBASE_ERR_ALLOC;
3062
3063 uref_free(upipe_ts_mux->flow_def_input);
3064 upipe_ts_mux->flow_def_input = flow_def_dup;
3065 upipe_ts_mux_conformance_guess(upipe);
3066 upipe_ts_mux_conformance_flow_def(upipe);
3067 return UBASE_ERR_NONE;
3068}

3085/** @internal @This sets the configured mtu.
3086 *
3087 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
3088 * @param mtu configured mtu, in octets
3089 * @return an error code
3090 */
3091static int upipe_ts_mux_set_output_size(struct upipe *upipe, unsigned int mtu)
3092{
3093 struct upipe_ts_mux *upipe_ts_mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
3094 if (unlikely(mtu < TS_SIZE)__builtin_expect(!!(mtu < 188),0))
3095 return UBASE_ERR_INVALID;
3096 mtu -= mtu % TS_SIZE188;
3097 upipe_ts_mux->mtu = mtu;
3098 if (upipe_ts_mux->total_octetrate)
3099 upipe_ts_mux->interval = (upipe_ts_mux->mtu * UCLOCK_FREQ27000000UL +
3100 upipe_ts_mux->total_octetrate - 1) /
3101 upipe_ts_mux->total_octetrate;
3102
3103 upipe_ts_mux->tb_size = T_STD_TS_BUFFER512 + mtu - TS_SIZE188;
3104
3105 struct uchain *uchain;
3106 ulist_foreach (&upipe_ts_mux->psi_pids, uchain)for ((uchain) = (&upipe_ts_mux->psi_pids)->next; (uchain
) != (&upipe_ts_mux->psi_pids); (uchain) = (uchain)->
next) {
3107 struct upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid *psi_pid =
3108 upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_from_uchain(uchain);
3109 upipe_ts_encaps_set_tb_size(psi_pid->encaps, upipe_ts_mux->tb_size);
3110 }
3111
3112 struct uchain *uchain_program;
3113 ulist_foreach (&upipe_ts_mux->programs, uchain_program)for ((uchain_program) = (&upipe_ts_mux->programs)->
next; (uchain_program) != (&upipe_ts_mux->programs); (
uchain_program) = (uchain_program)->next) {
3114 struct upipe_ts_mux_program *program =
3115 upipe_ts_mux_program_from_uchain(uchain_program);
3116 struct uchain *uchain_input;
3117 ulist_foreach (&program->inputs, uchain_input)for ((uchain_input) = (&program->inputs)->next; (uchain_input
) != (&program->inputs); (uchain_input) = (uchain_input
)->next) {
3118 struct upipe_ts_mux_input *input =
3119 upipe_ts_mux_input_from_uchain(uchain_input);
3120 upipe_ts_encaps_set_tb_size(input->encaps,
3121 upipe_ts_mux->tb_size);
3122 }
3123 }
3124 upipe_ts_mux_build_flow_def(upipe);
3125 return UBASE_ERR_NONE;
3126}

3128/** @internal @This returns the current conformance mode. It cannot
3129 * return CONFORMANCE_AUTO.
3130 *
3131 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
3132 * @param conformance_p filled in with the conformance
3133 * @return an error code
3134 */
3135static int _upipe_ts_mux_get_conformance(struct upipe *upipe,
3136 enum upipe_ts_conformance *conformance_p)
3137{
3138 struct upipe_ts_mux *upipe_ts_mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
3139 assert(conformance_p != NULL)((conformance_p != ((void*)0)) ? (void) (0) : __assert_fail (
"conformance_p != ((void*)0)", "upipe_ts_mux.c", 3139, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__
));
3140 *conformance_p = upipe_ts_mux->conformance;
3141 return UBASE_ERR_NONE;

3143
3144/** @internal @This sets the conformance mode.
3145 *
3146 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
3147 * @param conformance conformance mode
3148 * @return an error code
3149 */
3150static int _upipe_ts_mux_set_conformance(struct upipe *upipe,
3151 enum upipe_ts_conformance conformance)
3152{
3153 struct upipe_ts_mux *upipe_ts_mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
3154 switch (conformance) {
3155 case UPIPE_TS_CONFORMANCE_AUTO:
3156 upipe_ts_mux->auto_conformance = true1;
3157 upipe_ts_mux_conformance_guess(upipe);
3158 break;
3159 case UPIPE_TS_CONFORMANCE_ISO:
3160 case UPIPE_TS_CONFORMANCE_DVB:
3161 case UPIPE_TS_CONFORMANCE_DVB_NO_TABLES:
3162 case UPIPE_TS_CONFORMANCE_ATSC:
3163 case UPIPE_TS_CONFORMANCE_ISDB:
3164 upipe_ts_mux->auto_conformance = false0;
3165 upipe_ts_mux_conformance_change(upipe, conformance);
3166 break;
3167 default:
3168 return UBASE_ERR_INVALID;
3169 }
3170 return UBASE_ERR_NONE;
3171}

3391 uint64_t interval)
3392{
3393 struct upipe_ts_mux *upipe_ts_mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
3394 upipe_ts_mux->pcr_interval = interval;
3395
3396 struct uchain *uchain;
3397 ulist_foreach (&upipe_ts_mux->programs, uchain)for ((uchain) = (&upipe_ts_mux->programs)->next; (uchain
) != (&upipe_ts_mux->programs); (uchain) = (uchain)->
next) {
3398 struct upipe_ts_mux_program *program =
3399 upipe_ts_mux_program_from_uchain(uchain);
3400 upipe_ts_mux_set_pcr_interval(upipe_ts_mux_program_to_upipe(program),
3401 interval);
3402 }
3403 return UBASE_ERR_NONE;
3404}

3573/** @internal @This processes control commands on a ts_mux pipe.
3574 *
3575 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
3576 * @param command type of command to process
3577 * @param args arguments of the command
3578 * @return an error code
3579 */

3581{
3582 switch (command) {
3583 case UPIPE_ATTACH_UPUMP_MGR:
3584 upipe_ts_mux_set_upump(upipe, NULL((void*)0));
3585 return upipe_ts_mux_attach_upump_mgr(upipe);
3586 case UPIPE_ATTACH_UCLOCK:
3587 upipe_ts_mux_set_upump(upipe, NULL((void*)0));
3588 upipe_ts_mux_require_uclock(upipe);
3589 return UBASE_ERR_NONE;
3590 case UPIPE_GET_FLOW_DEF: {
3591 struct uref **p = va_arg(args, struct uref **)__builtin_va_arg(args, struct uref **);
3592 return upipe_ts_mux_get_flow_def(upipe, p);
3593 }
3594 case UPIPE_SET_FLOW_DEF: {

3596 return upipe_ts_mux_set_flow_def(upipe, flow_def);
3597 }
3598 case UPIPE_GET_OUTPUT: {

3600 return upipe_ts_mux_get_output(upipe, p);

3785/** @internal @This processes control commands on a ts_mux pipe, and
3786 * checks the status of the pipe afterwards.
3787 *
3788 * @param upipe description structure of the pipe
3789 * @param command type of command to process
3790 * @param args arguments of the command
3791 * @return an error code
3792 */
3793static int upipe_ts_mux_control(struct upipe *upipe, int command, va_list args)
3794{
3795 UBASE_RETURN(_upipe_ts_mux_control(upipe, command, args))do { int ubase_err_tmp = _upipe_ts_mux_control(upipe, command
, args); if (__builtin_expect(!!(!ubase_check(ubase_err_tmp))
,0)) return ubase_err_tmp; } while (0);;
3796
3797 return upipe_ts_mux_check(upipe, NULL((void*)0));
3798}
3799
3800/** @This frees a upipe.
3801 *
3802 * @param urefcount_real pointer to urefcount_real structure
3803 */
3804static void upipe_ts_mux_free(struct urefcount *urefcount_real)
3805{
3806 struct upipe_ts_mux *mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_urefcount_real(urefcount_real);
3807 struct upipe *upipe = upipe_ts_mux_to_upipe(mux);
3808
3809 if (mux->uref != NULL((void*)0)) {
3810 size_t uref_size;
3811 while ((ubase_check(uref_block_size(mux->uref, &uref_size)) &&
3812 uref_size < mux->mtu)) {
3813 struct ubuf *ubuf = ubuf_dup(mux->padding);
3814 if (ubuf == NULL((void*)0))
3815 break;
3816 upipe_ts_mux_append(upipe, ubuf, UINT64_MAX(18446744073709551615UL));
3817 }
3818
3819 upipe_ts_mux_complete(upipe, NULL((void*)0));
3820 }
3821
3822 upipe_throw_dead(upipe);
3823
3824 ubuf_free(mux->padding);
3825 uref_free(mux->flow_def_input);
3826 uprobe_clean(&mux->probe);
3827 urefcount_clean(urefcount_real);
3828 upipe_ts_mux_clean_inner_sink(upipe);
3829 upipe_ts_mux_clean_upump(upipe);
3830 upipe_ts_mux_clean_upump_mgr(upipe);
3831 upipe_ts_mux_clean_uref_mgr(upipe);
3832 upipe_ts_mux_clean_ubuf_mgr(upipe);
3833 upipe_ts_mux_clean_uclock(upipe);
3834 upipe_ts_mux_clean_output(upipe);
3835 upipe_ts_mux_clean_urefcount(upipe);
3836 upipe_ts_mux_free_void(upipe);
3837}

3843static void upipe_ts_mux_no_input(struct upipe *upipe)
3844{
3845 struct upipe_ts_mux *upipe_ts_mux = upipe_ts_mux_from_upipe(upipe);
3846
3847 upipe_ts_mux_clean_sub_programs(upipe);
3848 upipe_ts_mux_clean_bin_input(upipe);
3849 upipe_release(upipe_ts_mux->psig_nit);
3850 upipe_ts_mux->psig_nit = NULL((void*)0);
3851 upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_release(upipe_ts_mux->psi_pid_pat);
3852 upipe_ts_mux->psi_pid_pat = NULL((void*)0);
3853 upipe_release(upipe_ts_mux->sig);
3854 upipe_ts_mux->sig = NULL((void*)0);
3855 upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_release(upipe_ts_mux->psi_pid_nit);
3856 upipe_ts_mux->psi_pid_nit = NULL((void*)0);
3857 upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_release(upipe_ts_mux->psi_pid_sdt);
3858 upipe_ts_mux->psi_pid_sdt = NULL((void*)0);
3859 upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_release(upipe_ts_mux->psi_pid_eit);
3860 upipe_ts_mux->psi_pid_eit = NULL((void*)0);
3861 upipe_ts_mux_psi_pid_release(upipe_ts_mux->psi_pid_tdt);
3862 upipe_ts_mux->psi_pid_tdt = NULL((void*)0);

3866/** @This frees a upipe manager.
3867 *
3868 * @param urefcount pointer to urefcount structure
3869 */
3870static void upipe_ts_mux_mgr_free(struct urefcount *urefcount)
3871{
3872 struct upipe_ts_mux_mgr *ts_mux_mgr =
3873 upipe_ts_mux_mgr_from_urefcount(urefcount);
3874 upipe_mgr_release(ts_mux_mgr->ts_encaps_mgr);
3875 upipe_mgr_release(ts_mux_mgr->ts_tstd_mgr);
3876 upipe_mgr_release(ts_mux_mgr->ts_psi_join_mgr);
3877 upipe_mgr_release(ts_mux_mgr->ts_psig_mgr);
3878 upipe_mgr_release(ts_mux_mgr->ts_sig_mgr);
3879
3880 urefcount_clean(urefcount);
3881 free(ts_mux_mgr);
3882}

3884/** @This processes control commands on a ts_mux manager.
3885 *
3886 * @param mgr pointer to manager
3887 * @param command type of command to process
3888 * @param args arguments of the command
3889 * @return an error code
3890 */
3891static int upipe_ts_mux_mgr_control(struct upipe_mgr *mgr,
3892 int command, va_list args)
3893{
3894 struct upipe_ts_mux_mgr *ts_mux_mgr = upipe_ts_mux_mgr_from_upipe_mgr(mgr);
3895
3896 switch (command) {
3897#define GET_SET_MGR(name, NAME) \
3898 case UPIPE_TS_MUX_MGR_GET_##NAME##_MGR: { \
3899 UBASE_SIGNATURE_CHECK(args, UPIPE_TS_MUX_SIGNATURE){ if (__builtin_va_arg(args, unsigned int) != (((uint32_t)'t'
) | (((uint32_t)'s') << 8) | (((uint32_t)'m') << 16
) | (((uint32_t)'x') << 24))) return UBASE_ERR_UNHANDLED
; } \
3900 struct upipe_mgr **p = va_arg(args, struct upipe_mgr **)__builtin_va_arg(args, struct upipe_mgr **); \
3901 *p = ts_mux_mgr->name##_mgr; \
3902 return UBASE_ERR_NONE; \
3903 } \
3904 case UPIPE_TS_MUX_MGR_SET_##NAME##_MGR: { \
3905 UBASE_SIGNATURE_CHECK(args, UPIPE_TS_MUX_SIGNATURE){ if (__builtin_va_arg(args, unsigned int) != (((uint32_t)'t'
) | (((uint32_t)'s') << 8) | (((uint32_t)'m') << 16
) | (((uint32_t)'x') << 24))) return UBASE_ERR_UNHANDLED
; } \
3906 if (!urefcount_single(&ts_mux_mgr->urefcount)) \
3907 return UBASE_ERR_BUSY; \
3908 struct upipe_mgr *m = va_arg(args, struct upipe_mgr *)__builtin_va_arg(args, struct upipe_mgr *); \
3909 upipe_mgr_release(ts_mux_mgr->name##_mgr); \
3910 ts_mux_mgr->name##_mgr = upipe_mgr_use(m); \
3911 return UBASE_ERR_NONE; \
3912 }
3913
3914 GET_SET_MGR(ts_encaps, TS_ENCAPS)
3915 GET_SET_MGR(ts_tstd, TS_TSTD)
3916 GET_SET_MGR(ts_psi_join, TS_PSI_JOIN)
3917 GET_SET_MGR(ts_psig, TS_PSIG)
3918 GET_SET_MGR(ts_sig, TS_SIG)
3919#undef GET_SET_MGR
3920
3921 default:
3922 return UBASE_ERR_UNHANDLED;
3923 }
3924}

3926/** @This returns the management structure for all ts_mux pipes.
3927 *
3928 * @return pointer to manager
3929 */
3930struct upipe_mgr *upipe_ts_mux_mgr_alloc(void)
3931{
3932 struct upipe_ts_mux_mgr *ts_mux_mgr =
3933 malloc(sizeof(struct upipe_ts_mux_mgr));
3934 if (unlikely(ts_mux_mgr == NULL)__builtin_expect(!!(ts_mux_mgr == ((void*)0)),0))
3935 return NULL((void*)0);
3936
3937 ts_mux_mgr->ts_encaps_mgr = upipe_ts_encaps_mgr_alloc();
3938 ts_mux_mgr->ts_tstd_mgr = upipe_ts_tstd_mgr_alloc();
3939 ts_mux_mgr->ts_psi_join_mgr = upipe_ts_psi_join_mgr_alloc();
3940 ts_mux_mgr->ts_psig_mgr = upipe_ts_psig_mgr_alloc();
3941 ts_mux_mgr->ts_sig_mgr = upipe_ts_sig_mgr_alloc();
3942
3943 urefcount_init(upipe_ts_mux_mgr_to_urefcount(ts_mux_mgr),
3944 upipe_ts_mux_mgr_free);
3945 ts_mux_mgr->mgr.refcount = upipe_ts_mux_mgr_to_urefcount(ts_mux_mgr);
3946 ts_mux_mgr->mgr.signature = UPIPE_TS_MUX_SIGNATURE(((uint32_t)'t') | (((uint32_t)'s') << 8) | (((uint32_t
)'m') << 16) | (((uint32_t)'x') << 24));
3947 ts_mux_mgr->mgr.upipe_alloc = upipe_ts_mux_alloc;
3948 ts_mux_mgr->mgr.upipe_input = NULL((void*)0);
3949 ts_mux_mgr->mgr.upipe_control = upipe_ts_mux_control;
3950 ts_mux_mgr->mgr.upipe_mgr_control = upipe_ts_mux_mgr_control;
3951 return upipe_ts_mux_mgr_to_upipe_mgr(ts_mux_mgr);
3952}
